If you are looking to get a trailer to haul stuff, this is the place to get it done. We got an enclosed cargo trailer 12x6. My wife and I wanted a trailer like this for a long time. Trailer-plus asks you to put a $50 deposit down to reserve a trailer you are interested in so that others do not take it. < Text>
Walked by this spot a few times before finally stopping in, and I can see why there is always a huge lunch crowd here! This no-frills hot dog counter serves up a wonderful dog! I always forget how much I like a good hot dog, and I'm so thankful that I found Jimbo's to remind me! The owner was very nice and quick to help me. He just celebrated his 30th anniversary of business, and I see why he's been around so long. Top quality lunch on the cheap, I got a hot link with cheese the way I wanted it for less than $5! A new favorite lunch spot!</Text>

<UserId.>111557131120819189596< /UserId.><Review>Moving is easy and fun, said no one ever. We are 100% in that majority camp. With that said, Magali from StorQuest-Anaheim/Walnut was the highlight of our entire moving process.

I would go out on a limb to say that our experience with finding a new home, and subsequently moving, during a global pandemic was far from conventional. We were moving from DTLA to Anaheim and in the time of Covid, we were glad to make the normally 50-60 minute drive in half the time. Naturally, our luck ran out the weekend of our move when SoCal's economies reopened and it seemed like every car in LA/OC were on the streets and freeways at the same time. Being in bumper-to-bumper traffic usually sucks, but is exacerbated when driving a 15' U-Haul truck.

So we crawled to Anaheim, with me frantically on the phone with Magali half an hour before the office closed for us to rent our storage unit. She and I exchanged phone calls 3 times, with her on the other line being ever-so-patient, empathetic of the situation and willing to help the entire time. Although the storage unit was about to close, she was on the phone with her manager to try and accommodate us. Luckily, the manager was understanding and flexible, and allowed Magali to service us after working hours. Over the phone, she jumpstarted our application process so that all we had to do when we got to the office was pay and sign our lease. We realize that this is absolutely an exception, but in an unprecedented time, we all are experiencing our share of firsts.

When we got into the parking lot, I jumped out of the truck and ran into the office, where Magali was waiting for me. She was a sweetheart, and even more personable in person. 10 minutes later, we were starting to load up our storage unit.

The storage facility is new, clean and well-maintained, as was our unit. Access to the facility is open until 8PM (for those on the autopay plan), and when the gate closes. <username>Pricilla Dawson</username><date>1537248514192</date><rate>5</rate>< Review>
What I encountered was two very friendly staff who were funny, open, transparent, personable, obviously customer focused, and clearly happy to work for StorQuest.

My initial interaction with Martin Cazarez and Chris Naidu made all the difference.  The staff who represent a company make that first impression and set the tone which ultimately affects the outcome of the experience and sale.

Martin shared a brief history of his time with StorQuest and the success of the Anaheim location in the first month it opened.  Take note, storage space renters!  They're filling up fast here, so do yourself a favor and reserve your space ASAP.  You won't find another storage rental company  like this.  Clean, extended hours, a conference room (Free to reserve) for businesses that rent space, lots of equipment, lots of LIGHT (motion sensor activated), reasonable pricing, virtually tamper proof locks, and restrooms that are well kept too!

Chris Naidu was very funny and completely focused on my needs.  He showed genuine concern about getting me into the right space and interest in making it as easy as possible to move my things into a unit.

StorQuest sets the bar high for it‚Äôs competitors (the competition have a LOT of work to do), but the manager and staff who are essentially the face of StorQuest are setting StorQuest apart from the rest.</Review>
